<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:параллель.html>паралле́ль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">parallélʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:параллель.html>паралле́ли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:параллель.html>паралле́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:параллель.html>паралле́лей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geometry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> parallel (line)</li>
<li>parallel (line of latitude)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́ти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:город.html>города́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:находиться.html>нахо́дятся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одно́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:параллель.html>паралле́ли</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éti gorodá naxódjatsja na odnój <b>paralléli</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">These towns have the same latitude.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>parallel (line of reasoning similar to another one)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преподаватель.html>преподава́тель</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:провести.html>провёл</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:параллель.html>паралле́ль</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:между.html>ме́жду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́тими</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:факт.html>фа́ктами</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Prepodavátelʹ provjól <b>parallélʹ</b> méždu étimi fáktami.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The teacher established similarity between these facts.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:паранойя.html>парано́йя</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">paranójja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:паранойя.html>парано́йи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:паранойя.html>парано́йи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:паранойя.html>парано́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">pathology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> paranoia (a psychotic disorder characterized by delusions of persecution)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:парафин.html>парафи́н</a> (25596)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Paraffin</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***параша.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:параша.html>пара́ша</a> (13322)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:параша.html>пара́ша</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">paráša</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:параша.html>пара́ши</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:параша.html>пара́ши</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:параша.html>пара́ш</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>close-stool in a prison</li>
<li>bullshit, nonsense, untrue rumors</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The place near <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:параша.html>пара́ша</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">paráša</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is considered the least prestigious in Russian prison cells, which are often shared by many inmates. It is often reserved to the so called <i><a href = vnd.unilang:петух.html>петухи́</a></i>, passive homosexuals, the lowest standing caste in the Russian prison caste system. The word is therefore associated with something having very low quality. It can also be used in expressions such as <i><a href = vnd.unilang:твой.html>Твоё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>место</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:параша.html>пара́ши</a></i>, 'Your place is at the close-stool', which is considered utterly insulting.
</p>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:па.html>па</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ра́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ша.html>ша</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 4a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:парашют.html>парашю́т</a> (6907)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">parachute</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">para-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">protection against</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (as in <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">parasol</i>) and <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">chute</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fall</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:парашютист.html>парашюти́ст</a> (11324)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парашютист.html>парашюти́ст</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">parašutíst</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парашютист.html>парашюти́ста</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парашютист.html>парашюти́сты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парашютист.html>парашюти́стов</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парашютистка.html>парашюти́стка</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:паримый.html>па́римый</a> (7432)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:паримый.html>па́римый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">párimyj</span>)

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:па.html>па́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ри<span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-пар-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>.
</p>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0_3"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства_3"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:па.html>па</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ри́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4b.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-пар-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>.
</p>

***парк.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:парк.html>парк</a> (1758)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Park</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">park</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">parc</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парк.html>парк</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">park</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парк.html>па́рка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парк.html>па́рки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парк.html>па́рков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>park <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">for recreation</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́тот</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:парк.html>па́рк</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:знаменитый.html>знамени́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:статуя.html>ста́туями</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Étot <b>párk</b> znamenít svoími státujami.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">This <b>park</b> is famous for its statues.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>yard, depot</li>
<li>fleet, stock</li>
<li>depot</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:парк.html>парк</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">паркова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">parkovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парковка.html>парко́вка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">parkóvka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парковка.html>парко́вки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парковка.html>парко́вки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парковка.html>парко́вок</a></b>)

<ol><li>parking <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">space or action</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
